.. py:class:: AnimalBreedsCode(value)

   Bases: :py:obj:`spark_auto_mapper_fhir.value_sets.generic_type.GenericTypeCode`

   AnimalBreeds
   From: http://hl7.org/fhir/ValueSet/animal-breeds in valuesets.xml
       This example value set defines a set of codes that can be used to indicate
   breeds of species.

   .. py:attribute:: codeset
      :annotation: :spark_auto_mapper_fhir.fhir_types.uri.FhirUri = http://snomed.info/sct
